    <li> First let me stipulate that I am an Oz Naturals skin-care consumer and not only have tried almost every product in the line, I use most of their products every day and some of them both in the morning and in the evening as part of my nightly skin-care routine.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The first two products that initiated my appreciation of the Oz Naturals line is their Vitamin C 20% Amino Blend Hyaluronic Acid Serum, with the yellow square on the bottle and the second product is the Hyaluronic Acid Vitamin C, with a green square on the bottle.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have reached my sixties, and for the past, few months have started a rigorous and aggressive nightly procedure of derma rolling.  When I have finished with this procedure, my face is red, raw and my skin is extremely sensitive.  First, I apply the Oz Naturals Vitamin C Serum and it does NOT sting.  This was the only Vitamin C serum that had not irritated my face after this procedure, most likely because the others used alcohol content, whereas Oz Naturals uses Witch Hazel, which is not irritating on my skin.  After I have let the serum absorb for a moment or two and I feel the effect of a slight tightening, I then apply the Hyaluronic Acid.  The Hyaluronic Acid is a little thicker than the serum and it actually feels somewhat soothing to my raw skin.  Again, no sting at all.  I wait a moment or two for the Hyaluronic Acid to be completely absorbed and I can actually notice that the dry, raw skin is a little less red, and just a little plumped out.  Then I proceed to my nightly moisturizer.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It is in the morning that I get the pleasant surprise.  Overnight, my face has completely healed and the skin looks a little plumper and healthier.  I was not getting the same positive results before I started using Oz Naturals.  The morning results are definitely visible and I am positively thrilled that there is no irritation considering the abusive and aggressive nature that I am enduring with the derma rolling five nights a week.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I recommend both of these Oz Natural products, as a regular maintenance, for those who have sensitive skin issues, and for those of us who are going through any skin care treatments.  These products are gentle to the skin, and give positive results.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This ends my review of Oz Natural products - Hyaluronic Acid, however, for those who are just starting to learn about skin care maintenance, I have provided a brief synopsis of the benefits, functions, and the results of Hyaluronic Acid in general.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The Benefits of Hyaluronic Acid for Skin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Hyaluronic acid is an important natural component of skin produced by fibroblast skin cells, which decreases as we age.  Skin starts losing hyaluronic acid as early as age 18, but wrinkles and other skin damage from hyaluronic acid loss generally do not show up until we are in our late 30s or early 40s.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Hyaluronic acid, also known as HA, is a natural compound found in skin that has many important functions; including holding in moisture, providing cushioning, aiding in tissue repair, holding together the skin structural components collagen and elastin, and helping create a protective barrier against microorganisms.  The topical HA product is considered effective at moisturizing surface skin cells, which prevents water loss and protects the skin from dirt and other pollutants.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Moisturizing - Since hyaluronic acid holds moisture well--holding up to 1,000 times its weight in water--it functions not only to deliver water to the skin, but also to hold it there.  As a large molecule, it does not permeate deep into the skin, but instead stays near the surface where it moisturizes the skin&#x27;s outer surface layers.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Wrinkles - The loss of natural hyaluronic acid is one of the causes of wrinkles, so the idea of putting HA back into the skin to repair wrinkles makes sense.  Since topical HA cannot penetrate to deeper layers, the moisturizing effects will only last a fewdays.  Repeated use will maintain moisture levels in the skin, preventing skin dehydration.  Hyaluronic acid is useful for reducing or removing wrinkles.  By reducing wrinkles, hyaluronic acid does help to produce healthier skin, restoring skin tone, for a smooth and supple young and healthier look.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I really hope that this review and/or the general information has been informative, because skin care can be a little confusing in the functions of each product, so hopefully this has been helpful.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;UPDATE;  6/06/14  HELPFUL TIP&lt;br /&gt;I live in the desert, the climate is so dry with almost no humidity.  Keeping moisturized is a challenge here and we know that dry skin is very prone to wrinkles.  Anyway, I recently purchased a humidifier for my bedroom, which is where I spend 8-10 hours from evening to morning.  It has made a substantial difference in my skin, in the range of about 15% - 20%, a little different each day.  So, if you reside in a relatively dry and low humidity area, try using a humidifier, the benefits of skin care products are improved.days.  Repeated use will maintain moisture levels in the skin, preventing skin dehydration.  Hyaluronic acid is useful for reducing or removing wrinkles.     <li> This is a great product. It comes highly recommended. But don&#x27;t be misled by the 100% pure Hyaluronic acid. What they mean is 100% of a 1% solution. Pure 100% Hyaluronic acid is a powder. It would take tons of liquid to dissolve into a serum. Even 25% Hyaluronic acid would be a thick paste, and it would be horribly destructive to your skin. A 1% solution is the standard amount used by practically all manufacturers. It is proven to give the best results. The other 99% of the serum is made up of other ingredients that vary by manufacturer (vitamin C, E, aloe vera, emolients, etc,) As long as you can trust that it is a 1% solution (best to choose the vegan/vegetarian type, the non vegan/vegetarian type is made out of the roosters&#x27; combs, among other things), they&#x27;re all pretty much the same. Don&#x27;t be misled by all the hype and the price. Also, most people don&#x27;t know that Hyaluroic Acid can be taken internally (as capsules or as a powder, a very small amount dissolved into your favorite beverage). Internally, it is used to improve the appearance of your skin and, especially, to improve joint health. In your joints it pulls moisture into the joints, which has a lubricating effect. (Search for Hyaluronic capsules or Hyaluronic powder here on Amazon). You can even make your own serum from the powder, it comes with the instructions on how to do this. This is what I do, because it is much, much cheaper. You can even create your own Hyaluronic Acid at home if you&#x27;re so inclined. Check out how to do this on YouTube)</li>

That sticky sensation dissipates after a minute or two of drying. The serum is a lovely consistency; liquidity enough that it&#x27;s easy to apply and move around your face but gel enough that it doesn&#x27;t run all over the place before you&#x27;ve had a chance to apply it. It has a very slight scent, but it&#x27;s really pleasant; I detect rose which is a smell I&#x27;m always happy to have in my beauty products but I know there are just as many people who hate the smell as there are that love it. You have to work with it very quickly because as soon as it comes into contact with your skin it sinks in, something that I love about it, it makes my skin care routine very fast. Firstly I cleanse and tone my face as usual, then I apply the serum. As soon as it&#x27;s been applied there is no residue on the skin at all, within a couple of seconds it&#x27;s completely disappeared and you&#x27;re ready for your moisturiser. I use this all over my face, even up to my lash line on my eyes, and it doesn&#x27;t sting or affect my sensitive eyes in any way, it even helps my eye cream to not effect them, something I really wasn&#x27;t expecting. There isn&#x27;t one point there that I can disagree with. Now about the serum: in the past I have used products containing hyaluronic acid, but apart from how much active ingredient is actually in the bottle, it seems that the synergy with other components is crucial. This serum is packaged in a glass bottle with a dropper to facilitate precise application. The contents are 1 fluid ounce or 30 ml, which is pretty standard, but you need very little to cover your whole face and neck, making this product really good value for money. It looks like it can easily last a couple of months.  With gentle massage, the almost clear gel sinks in easily and dries quickly. You then apply your favourite cream or oil on top, which now has a much better chance to penetrate and actually do some of the wonderful things promised on the box.
